# ::id 1
# ::idiom break someone's heart
# ::snt ' Go on, my love, ' she used to whisper in Estella's ear, ' break men's hearts and have no mercy!
# ::usage figurative
(s / say-01
      :ARG0 (ii / i)
      :ARG1 (g / go-on-15
            :mode imperative
            :ARG1-of (l / love-01
                  :ARG0 ii))
      :ARG2 (w / whisper-01
            :ARG0 (s2 / she
                  :part (e / ear))
            :ARG1 (a / and
                  :op1 (b / break-heart-31
                        :ARG1 (m / man))
                  :op2 (m2 / mercy
                        :polarity -))
            :ARG2 (p / person
                  :name (n / name
                        :op1 "Estella")
                  :part e)
            :time (u / use-03)))

# ::id 3
# ::idiom ring a bell

# ::snt From 1935 Noel was increasingly oppressed by the diabetes from which he suffered, blindness, and a cancerous growth, but nothing could dampen his spirits, and when he could no longer sing the liturgy, he learned it off by heart.
# ::usage figurative
(c / contrast-01
      :ARG1 (o / oppress-01
            :ARG0 (d / diabetes
                  :ARG1-of (s / suffer-01
                        :ARG0 (p / person
                              :name (n / name
                                    :op1 "Noel"))))
            :ARG1 p
            :ARG1-of (ii / increase-01)
            :time (d2 / date-entity
                  :year 1935))
      :ARG2 (a / and
            :op1 (p2 / possible-01
                  :polarity -
                  :ARG1 (d3 / dampen-01
                        :ARG0 (n2 / nothing)
                        :ARG1 (s2 / spirit
                              :poss p)))
            :op2 (l / learn-01
                  :ARG0 p
                  :ARG1 (ii2 / it)
                  :manner (b / by-heart)
                  :time (p3 / possible-01
                        :ARG1 (s3 / sing-01
                              :ARG0 p
                              :ARG1 (l2 / liturgy)
                              :time (n3 / no-longer))))))
